</div>
<p>As of 2010<sup class="plainlinks noprint asof-tag update" style="display:none;"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Jacksonville,_Florida&amp;action=edit">[update]</a></sup>, those of Hispanic or Latino ancestry accounted for 7.7% of Jacksonville's population. Out of the 7.7%, 2.6% <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Puerto_Rican_people" title="Puerto Rican people">Puerto Rican</a>, 1.7% <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mexican_people" title="Mexican people">Mexican</a>, and 0.9% were <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Cuban_people" title="Cuban people">Cuban</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-HiLaJax_105-0"><a href="#cite_note-HiLaJax-105">[103]</a></sup></p>
<p>As of 2010<sup class="plainlinks noprint asof-tag update" style="display:none;"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Jacksonville,_Florida&amp;action=edit">[update]</a></sup>, those of African ancestry accounted for 30.7% of Jacksonville's population, which includes <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/African_American" title="African American">African Americans</a>. Out of the 30.7%, 1.8% were <a href="/wiki/Sub-Saharan_Africa" title="Sub-Saharan Africa">Sub-Saharan Africa</a>, 1.4% were <a href="/wiki/West_Indian" title="West Indian">West Indian</a> or <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Afro-Caribbean_American" title="Afro-Caribbean American">Afro-Caribbean American</a> (0.5% <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Haitian_people" title="Haitian people">Haitian</a>, 0.4% <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Jamaican_people" title="Jamaican people">Jamaican</a>, 0.1% <a href="/wiki/Afro-Caribbean" title="Afro-Caribbean">Other or Unspecified West Indian</a>, 0.1% <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Bahamian_people" title="Bahamian people">Bahamian</a>, 0.1% <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Barbadian_people" title="Barbadian people">Barbadian</a>), and 0.6% were <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Black_Hispanic" title="Black Hispanic">Black Hispanics</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-HiLaJax_105-1"><a href="#cite_note-HiLaJax-105">[103]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-JAXpop_106-0"><a href="#cite_note-JAXpop-106">[104]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-JAXdemo_107-0"><a href="#cite_note-JAXdemo-107">[105]</a></sup></p>
<p>As of 2010<sup class="plainlinks noprint asof-tag update" style="display:none;"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Jacksonville,_Florida&amp;action=edit">[update]</a></sup>, those of (non-Hispanic white) European ancestry accounted for 55.1% of Jacksonville's population. Out of the 55.1%, 10.4% were <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/German_people" title="German people">German</a>, 10.2% <a href="/wiki/Irish_people" title="Irish people">Irish</a>, 8.8% <a href="/wiki/English_people" title="English people">English</a>, 3.9% <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Italian_people" title="Italian people">Italian</a>, 2.2% <a href="/wiki/French_people" title="French people">French</a>, 2.0% <a href="/wiki/Scottish_people" title="Scottish people">Scottish</a>, 2.0% <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Scotch-Irish_American" title="Scotch-Irish American">Scotch-Irish</a>, 1.7% <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Polish_people" title="Polish people">Polish</a>, 1.1% <a href="/wiki/Dutch_people" title="Dutch people">Dutch</a>, 0.6% <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Russian_people" title="Russian people">Russian</a>, 0.5% <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Norwegian_people" title="Norwegian people">Norwegian</a>, 0.5% <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Swedish_people" title="Swedish people">Swedish</a>, 0.5% <a href="/wiki/Welsh_people" title="Welsh people">Welsh</a>, and 0.5% were <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/French_Canadian_people" title="French Canadian people">French Canadian</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-JAXdemo_107-1"><a href="#cite_note-JAXdemo-107">[105]</a></sup></p>
<p>As of 2010<sup class="plainlinks noprint asof-tag update" style="display:none;"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Jacksonville,_Florida&amp;action=edit">[update]</a></sup>, those of Asian ancestry accounted for 4.3% of Jacksonville's population. Out of the 4.3%, 1.8% <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Filipino_people" title="Filipino people">Filipino</a>, 0.9% were <a href="/wiki/Indian_people" title="Indian people">Indian</a>, 0.6% <a href="/wiki/Asian_people" title="Asian people">Other Asian</a>, 0.5% <a href="/wiki/Vietnamese_people" title="Vietnamese people">Vietnamese</a>, 0.3% <a href="/wiki/Chinese_people" title="Chinese people">Chinese</a>, 0.2% <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Korean_people" title="Korean people">Korean</a>, and 0.1% were <a href="/wiki/Japanese_people" title="Japanese people">Japanese</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-JAXdemo_107-2"><a href="#cite_note-JAXdemo-107">[105]</a></sup></p>
<p>In 2010, 6.7% of the population considered themselves to be of only <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/American_people" title="American people">American</a> ancestry (regardless of race or ethnicity.)<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-JAXpop_106-1"><a href="#cite_note-JAXpop-106">[104]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-JAXdemo_107-3"><a href="#cite_note-JAXdemo-107">[105]</a></sup> And 0.9% were of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Arab_people" title="Arab people">Arab</a> ancestry, as of 2010<sup class="plainlinks noprint asof-tag update" style="display:none;"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Jacksonville,_Florida&amp;action=edit">[update]</a></sup>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-JAXdemo_107-4"><a href="#cite_note-JAXdemo-107">[105]</a></sup></p>
<p>As of 2010<sup class="plainlinks noprint asof-tag update" style="display:none;"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Jacksonville,_Florida&amp;action=edit">[update]</a></sup>, there were 366,273 households out of which 11.8% were vacant. 23.9% of households had children under the age of 18 living with them, 43.8% were <a href="/wiki/Marriage" title="Marriage">married couples</a>, 15.2% had a female householder with no husband present, and 36.4% were non-families. 29.7% of all households were made up of individuals and 7.9% had someone living alone who was 65 years of age or older. The average household size was 2.55 and the average family size was 3.21. In the city, the population was spread out with 23.9% under the age of 18, 10.5% from 18 to 24, 28.5% from 25 to 44, 26.2% from 45 to 64, and 10.9% who were 65 years of age or older. The median age was 35.5 years. For every 100 females there were 94.1 males. For every 100 females age 18 and over, there were 91.3 males.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-JAXdemo_107-5"><a href="#cite_note-JAXdemo-107">[105]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-JAXage_108-0"><a href="#cite_note-JAXage-108">[106]</a></sup></p>
<p>In 2010, the median income for a household in the county was $48,829, and the median income for a family was $59,272. Males had a median income of $42,485 versus $34,209 for females. The <a href="/wiki/Per_capita_income" title="Per capita income">per capita income</a> for the county was $25,227. About 10.5% of families and 14.3% of the population were below the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Poverty_line" title="Poverty line">poverty line</a>, including 20.4% of those under age 18 and 9.9% of those aged 65 or over.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-109"><a href="#cite_note-109">[107]</a></sup></p>
<p>In 2010, 9.2% of the county's population was <a href="/wiki/Foreign_born" title="Foreign born">foreign born</a>, with 49.6% being <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Naturalized_citizen_of_the_United_States" title="Naturalized citizen of the United States">naturalized American citizens</a>. Of foreign born residents, 38.0% were born in <a href="/wiki/Latin_America" title="Latin America">Latin America</a>, 35.7% born in <a href="/wiki/Asia" title="Asia">Asia</a>, 17.9% were born in <a href="/wiki/Europe" title="Europe">Europe</a>, 5.9% born in <a href="/wiki/Africa" title="Africa">Africa</a>, 1.9% in <a href="/wiki/North_America" title="North America">North America</a>, and 0.5% were born in <a href="/wiki/Oceania" title="Oceania">Oceania</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-JAXdemo_107-6"><a href="#cite_note-JAXdemo-107">[105]</a></sup></p>
<p>As of 2010<sup class="plainlinks noprint asof-tag update" style="display:none;"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Jacksonville,_Florida&amp;action=edit">[update]</a></sup>, 87.1% of Jacksonville's population age five and over spoke only <a href="/wiki/English_language" title="English language">English</a> at home while 5.8% of the population spoke <a href="/wiki/Spanish_language" title="Spanish language">Spanish</a> at home. About 3.3% spoke other <a href="/wiki/Indo-European_languages" title="Indo-European languages">Indo-European languages</a> at home. About 2.9% spoke <a href="/wiki/Languages_of_Asia" title="Languages of Asia">Asian languages</a> or <a href="/wiki/Languages_of_Oceania" title="Languages of Oceania">Pacific Islander languages</a>/<a href="/wiki/Oceanic_languages" title="Oceanic languages">Oceanic languages</a> at home. The remaining 0.9% of the population spoke <a href="/wiki/Language" title="Language">other languages</a> at home. In total, 12.9% spoke another language other than English.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-JAXdemo_107-7"><a href="#cite_note-JAXdemo-107">[105]</a></sup></p>
<p>As of 2000, speakers of English as a <a href="/wiki/First_language" title="First language">first language</a> accounted for 90.60% of all residents, while those who spoke <a href="/wiki/Spanish_language" title="Spanish language">Spanish</a> made up 4.13%, <a href="/wiki/Tagalog_language" title="Tagalog language">Tagalog</a> 1.00%, <a href="/wiki/French_language" title="French language">French</a> 0.47%, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Arabic_language" title="Arabic language">Arabic</a> 0.44%, <a href="/wiki/German_language" title="German language">German</a> 0.43%, <a href="/wiki/Vietnamese_language" title="Vietnamese language">Vietnamese</a> at 0.31%, <a href="/wiki/Russian_language" title="Russian language">Russian</a> was 0.21% and <a href="/wiki/Italian_language" title="Italian language">Italian</a> made up 0.17% of the population.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-110"><a href="#cite_note-110">[108]</a></sup></p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Religion">Religion</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Jacksonville,_Florida&amp;action=edit&amp;section=17" title="Edit section: Religion">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Jacksonville has a diverse religious population. The largest religious group is <a href="/wiki/Protestantism" title="Protestantism">Protestant</a>. According to the <a href="/wiki/Association_of_Religion_Data_Archives" title="Association of Religion Data Archives">Association of Religion Data Archives</a> (ARDA), in 2010 the Jacksonville metropolitan area had an estimated 365,267 <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Evangelical_Protestant" title="Evangelical Protestant">Evangelical Protestants</a>, 76,100 <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mainline_Protestants" title="Mainline Protestants">Mainline Protestants</a>, and 56,769 <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Black_Protestant" title="Black Protestant">Black Protestants</a>, though figures for the latter were incomplete. There were around 1200 Protestant congregations in various denominations.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-ARDA_111-0"><a href="#cite_note-ARDA-111">[109]</a></sup> Notable Protestant churches include <a href="/wiki/Bethel_Baptist_Institutional_Church" title="Bethel Baptist Institutional Church">Bethel Baptist Institutional Church</a> and <a href="/wiki/First_Baptist_Church_of_Jacksonville" title="First Baptist Church of Jacksonville">First Baptist Church</a>, the city's oldest Baptist churches. The <a href="/wiki/Episcopal_Diocese_of_Florida" title="Episcopal Diocese of Florida">Episcopal Diocese of Florida</a> has its <a href="/wiki/Episcopal_see" title="Episcopal see">see</a> at <a href="/wiki/St._John%27s_Cathedral_(Jacksonville)" title="St. John's Cathedral (Jacksonville)">St. John's Cathedral</a>, the current building dating to 1906.</p>
<p>Jacksonville is part of the <a href="/wiki/Catholic_Church" title="Catholic Church">Catholic</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Diocese_of_St._Augustine" title="Diocese of St. Augustine">Diocese of St. Augustine</a>, which covers seventeen counties in North Florida.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-112"><a href="#cite_note-112">[110]</a></sup> ARDA estimated 133,155 Catholics attending 25 parishes in the Jacksonville metropolitan area in 2010.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-ARDA_111-1"><a href="#cite_note-ARDA-111">[109]</a></sup> One notable Catholic church in Jacksonville is the <a href="/wiki/Basilica_of_the_Immaculate_Conception_(Jacksonville)" title="Basilica of the Immaculate Conception (Jacksonville)">Basilica of the Immaculate Conception</a>, a <a href="/wiki/Minor_basilica" title="Minor basilica">minor basilica</a> added to the <a href="/wiki/National_Register_of_Historic_Places" title="National Register of Historic Places">National Register of Historic Places</a> in 1992.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-113"><a href="#cite_note-113">[111]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-114"><a href="#cite_note-114">[112]</a></sup> There are also two <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Eastern_Catholic" title="Eastern Catholic">Eastern Catholic</a> parishes, one of the <a href="/wiki/Syriac_Catholic_Church" title="Syriac Catholic Church">Syriac Catholic Church</a> and one of the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Maronite_Church" title="Maronite Church">Maronite Church</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-115"><a href="#cite_note-115">[113]</a></sup> According to ARDA, in 2010 there were 2520 <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Eastern_Orthodox" title="Eastern Orthodox">Eastern Orthodox</a> Christians representing four churches in the Eastern Orthodox communion, as well as congregations of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Syriac_Orthodox" title="Syriac Orthodox">Syriac Orthodox</a>, <a href="/wiki/Armenian_Apostolic_Church" title="Armenian Apostolic Church">Armenian Apostolic</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ethiopian_Orthodox" title="Ethiopian Orthodox">Ethiopian Orthodox</a>, and <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Coptic_Orthodox" title="Coptic Orthodox">Coptic Orthodox</a> Christians.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-ARDA_111-2"><a href="#cite_note-ARDA-111">[109]</a></sup></p>
<p>ARDA also estimated 14,886 members of <a href="/wiki/The_Church_of_Jesus_Christ_of_Latter-day_Saints" title="The Church of Jesus Christ of Latter-day Saints">The Church of Jesus Christ of Latter-day Saints</a> (LDS Church) and 511 <a href="/wiki/Unitarian_Universalism" title="Unitarian Universalism">Unitarian Universalists</a> in 2010.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-ARDA_111-3"><a href="#cite_note-ARDA-111">[109]</a></sup> There were an estimated 8,581 <a href="/wiki/Islam" title="Islam">Muslims</a> attending seven mosques, the largest being the Islamic Center of Northeast Florida.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-ARDA_111-4"><a href="#cite_note-ARDA-111">[109]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-116"><a href="#cite_note-116">[114]</a></sup> The <a href="/wiki/Jews" title="Jews">Jewish</a> community, which numbered 6,028 in 2010,<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-ARDA_111-5"><a href="#cite_note-ARDA-111">[109]</a></sup> is largely centered in the neighborhood of <a href="/wiki/Mandarin_(Jacksonville)" title="Mandarin (Jacksonville)">Mandarin</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-117"><a href="#cite_note-117">[115]</a></sup> There are five <a href="/wiki/Orthodox_Judaism" title="Orthodox Judaism">Orthodox</a>, two <a href="/wiki/Reform_Judaism" title="Reform Judaism">Reform</a>, two <a href="/wiki/Conservative_Judaism" title="Conservative Judaism">Conservative</a>, and one <a href="/wiki/Reconstructionist_Judaism" title="Reconstructionist Judaism">Reconstructionist</a> synagogues. The <a href="/wiki/Rohr_Jewish_Learning_Institute" title="Rohr Jewish Learning Institute">Rohr Jewish Learning Institute</a> teaches courses for the community.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-ARDA_111-6"><a href="#cite_note-ARDA-111">[109]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-118"><a href="#cite_note-118">[116]</a></sup></p>
<p>ARDA also estimated 4,595 <a href="/wiki/Hinduism" title="Hinduism">Hindus</a>, 3,530 <a href="/wiki/Buddhism" title="Buddhism">Buddhists</a> and 650 <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Bah%C3%A1%27%C3%AD" title="Bahá'í">Bahá'ís</a> in the Jacksonville area in 2010.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-ARDA_111-7"><a href="#cite_note-ARDA-111">[109]</a></sup></p>
<ul class="gallery mw-gallery-traditional">
<li class="gallerybox" style="width: 155px">
<div style="width: 155px">
<div class="thumb" style="width: 150px;">
